 1977   /* Function Definitions */
 1978   static void cornerOrientations(const emlrtStack *sp, const emxArray_real32_T
 1979     *Ix2, const emxArray_real32_T *Iy2, const emxArray_real32_T *Ixy, const
 1980     real32_T p[2], real32_T v1[2], real32_T v2[2])
 1981   {
 1982     int32_T sgn1;
 1983     int32_T sgn2;
 1984     real32_T df;
 1985     real32_T adf;
 1986     real32_T tb;
 1987     real32_T ab;
 1988     real32_T tn;
 1989     boolean_T b_p;
 1990     real32_T sn1[2];
 1991     real32_T cs1[2];
 1992     static const real32_T fv0[4] = { 0.707106769F, 0.707106769F, -0.707106769F,
 1993       0.707106769F };
 1994   
 1995     emlrtStack st;
 1996     emlrtStack b_st;
 1997     emlrtStack c_st;
 1998     st.prev = sp;
 1999     st.tls = sp->tls;
 2000     b_st.prev = &st;
 2001     b_st.tls = st.tls;
 2002     c_st.prev = &b_st;
 2003     c_st.tls = b_st.tls;
 2004     sgn1 = Ix2->size[0];
 2005     sgn2 = (int32_T)p[1];
 2006     if (!((sgn2 >= 1) && (sgn2 <= sgn1))) {
 2007       emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(sgn2, 1, sgn1, &mb_emlrtBCI, sp);
 2008     }
 2009   
 2010     sgn1 = Ix2->size[1];
 2011     sgn2 = (int32_T)p[0];
 2012     if (!((sgn2 >= 1) && (sgn2 <= sgn1))) {
 2013       emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(sgn2, 1, sgn1, &nb_emlrtBCI, sp);
 2014     }
 2015   
 2016     sgn1 = Ixy->size[0];
 2017     sgn2 = (int32_T)p[1];
 2018     if (!((sgn2 >= 1) && (sgn2 <= sgn1))) {
 2019       emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(sgn2, 1, sgn1, &ob_emlrtBCI, sp);
 2020     }
 2021   
 2022     sgn1 = Ixy->size[1];
 2023     sgn2 = (int32_T)p[0];
 2024     if (!((sgn2 >= 1) && (sgn2 <= sgn1))) {
 2025       emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(sgn2, 1, sgn1, &pb_emlrtBCI, sp);
 2026     }
 2027   
 2028     sgn1 = Iy2->size[0];
 2029     sgn2 = (int32_T)p[1];
 2030     if (!((sgn2 >= 1) && (sgn2 <= sgn1))) {
 2031       emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(sgn2, 1, sgn1, &qb_emlrtBCI, sp);
 2032     }
 2033   
 2034     sgn1 = Iy2->size[1];
 2035     sgn2 = (int32_T)p[0];
 2036     if (!((sgn2 >= 1) && (sgn2 <= sgn1))) {
 2037       emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(sgn2, 1, sgn1, &rb_emlrtBCI, sp);
 2038     }
 2039   
 2040     df = Ix2->data[((int32_T)p[1] + Ix2->size[0] * ((int32_T)p[0] - 1)) - 1] -
 2041       Iy2->data[((int32_T)p[1] + Iy2->size[0] * ((int32_T)p[0] - 1)) - 1];
 2042     adf = muSingleScalarAbs(df);
 2043     tb = Ixy->data[((int32_T)p[1] + Ixy->size[0] * ((int32_T)p[0] - 1)) - 1] +
 2044       Ixy->data[((int32_T)p[1] + Ixy->size[0] * ((int32_T)p[0] - 1)) - 1];
 2045     ab = muSingleScalarAbs(tb);
 2046     if (adf > ab) {
 2047       tn = ab / adf;
 2048       st.site = &ef_emlrtRSI;
 2049       b_st.site = &if_emlrtRSI;
 2050       st.site = &ef_emlrtRSI;
 2051       adf *= muSingleScalarSqrt(1.0F + tn * tn);
 2052     } else if (adf < ab) {
 2053       tn = adf / ab;
 2054       st.site = &ff_emlrtRSI;
 2055       b_st.site = &if_emlrtRSI;
 2056       st.site = &ff_emlrtRSI;
 2057       adf = ab * muSingleScalarSqrt(1.0F + tn * tn);
 2058     } else {
 2059       adf = ab * 1.41421354F;
 2060     }
 2061   
 2062     if (Ix2->data[((int32_T)p[1] + Ix2->size[0] * ((int32_T)p[0] - 1)) - 1] +
 2063         Iy2->data[((int32_T)p[1] + Iy2->size[0] * ((int32_T)p[0] - 1)) - 1] < 0.0F)
 2064     {
 2065       sgn1 = -1;
 2066     } else {
 2067       sgn1 = 1;
 2068     }
 2069   
 2070     if (df > 0.0F) {
 2071       adf += df;
 2072       sgn2 = 1;
 2073     } else {
 2074       adf = df - adf;
 2075       sgn2 = -1;
 2076     }
 2077   
 2078     if (muSingleScalarAbs(adf) > ab) {
 2079       tn = -tb / adf;
 2080       st.site = &gf_emlrtRSI;
 2081       adf = 1.0F + tn * tn;
 2082       b_p = (adf < 0.0F);
 2083       if (b_p) {
 2084         b_st.site = &jf_emlrtRSI;
 2085         c_st.site = &jf_emlrtRSI;
 2086         b_error(&c_st);
 2087       }
 2088   
 2089       df = 1.0F / muSingleScalarSqrt(adf);
 2090       adf = tn * df;
 2091     } else if (ab == 0.0F) {
 2092       adf = 1.0F;
 2093       df = 0.0F;
 2094     } else {
 2095       tn = -adf / tb;
 2096       st.site = &hf_emlrtRSI;
 2097       adf = 1.0F + tn * tn;
 2098       b_p = (adf < 0.0F);
 2099       if (b_p) {
 2100         b_st.site = &jf_emlrtRSI;
 2101         c_st.site = &jf_emlrtRSI;
 2102         b_error(&c_st);
 2103       }
 2104   
 2105       adf = 1.0F / muSingleScalarSqrt(adf);
 2106       df = tn * adf;
 2107     }
 2108   
 2109     if (sgn1 == sgn2) {
 2110       tn = adf;
 2111       adf = -df;
 2112       df = tn;
 2113     }
 2114   
 2115     sn1[0] = -df;
 2116     sn1[1] = adf;
 2117     cs1[0] = adf;
 2118     cs1[1] = df;
 2119     for (sgn1 = 0; sgn1 < 2; sgn1++) {
 2120       v1[sgn1] = 0.0F;
 2121       v2[sgn1] = 0.0F;
 2122       for (sgn2 = 0; sgn2 < 2; sgn2++) {
 2123         v1[sgn1] += sn1[sgn2] * fv0[sgn2 + (sgn1 << 1)];
 2124         v2[sgn1] += cs1[sgn2] * fv0[sgn2 + (sgn1 << 1)];
 2125       }
 2126     }
 2127   }

 2266         nonSingletonDimFound = false;

 2268           nonSingletonDimFound = true;
 2269         }
 2270   
 2271         if (nonSingletonDimFound) {
 2272           nonSingletonDimFound = true;
 2273         } else {

 2275         }
 2276       } else {
 2277         nonSingletonDimFound = false;
 2278       }
 2279

 3670   
 3671   static void poly2RectMask(const emlrtStack *sp, real_T b_X[4], real_T Y[4],
 3672     real_T height, real_T width, emxArray_boolean_T *mask)
 3673   {
 3674     int32_T i32;
 3675     int32_T loop_ub;
 3676     int32_T i33;
 3677     int32_T i34;
 3678     int32_T i35;
 3679     int32_T unnamed_idx_0;
 3680     emlrtStack st;
 3681     emlrtStack b_st;
 3682     st.prev = sp;
 3683     st.tls = sp->tls;
 3684     st.site = &wi_emlrtRSI;
 3685     b_st.prev = &st;
 3686     b_st.tls = st.tls;
 3687     b_st.site = &yi_emlrtRSI;
 3688     c_sort(&b_st, b_X);
 3689     st.site = &xi_emlrtRSI;
 3690     b_st.site = &yi_emlrtRSI;
 3691     c_sort(&b_st, Y);
 3692     i32 = mask->size[0] * mask->size[1];
 3693     mask->size[0] = (int32_T)height;
 3694     mask->size[1] = (int32_T)width;
 3695     emxEnsureCapacity_boolean_T(sp, mask, i32, &ck_emlrtRTEI);
 3696     loop_ub = (int32_T)height * (int32_T)width;
 3697     for (i32 = 0; i32 < loop_ub; i32++) {
 3698       mask->data[i32] = false;
 3699     }
 3700   
 3701     if (Y[1] > Y[2]) {
 3702       i33 = 1;
 3703       i32 = 1;
 3704     } else {
 3705       if (Y[1] != (int32_T)muDoubleScalarFloor(Y[1])) {
 3706         emlrtIntegerCheckR2012b(Y[1], &cc_emlrtDCI, sp);
 3707       }
 3708   
 3709       i32 = (int32_T)height;
 3710       i33 = (int32_T)Y[1];
 3711       if (!((i33 >= 1) && (i33 <= i32))) {
 3712         emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(i33, 1, i32, &uh_emlrtBCI, sp);
 3713       }
 3714   
 3715       if (Y[2] != (int32_T)muDoubleScalarFloor(Y[2])) {
 3716         emlrtIntegerCheckR2012b(Y[2], &dc_emlrtDCI, sp);
 3717       }
 3718   
 3719       i32 = (int32_T)height;
 3720       i35 = (int32_T)Y[2];
 3721       if (!((i35 >= 1) && (i35 <= i32))) {
 3722         emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(i35, 1, i32, &vh_emlrtBCI, sp);
 3723       }
 3724   
 3725       i32 = i35 + 1;
 3726     }
 3727   
 3728     if (b_X[1] > b_X[2]) {
 3729       i34 = 1;
 3730       i35 = 1;
 3731     } else {
 3732       if (b_X[1] != (int32_T)muDoubleScalarFloor(b_X[1])) {
 3733         emlrtIntegerCheckR2012b(b_X[1], &ec_emlrtDCI, sp);
 3734       }
 3735   
 3736       i35 = (int32_T)width;
 3737       i34 = (int32_T)b_X[1];
 3738       if (!((i34 >= 1) && (i34 <= i35))) {
 3739         emlrtDynamicBoundsCheckR2012b(i34, 1, i35, &wh_emlrtBCI, sp);
 3740       }
 3741
